<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wachten.html>wachte</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wahta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wahtwō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wacht.html>wacht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wachten.html>wachten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wacht.html>wachtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>guard-post</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***wanneer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wanneer.html>wanneer</a> (255)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wanneer.html>wanneer</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wan eer</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wan ēr</i>. The former part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> found as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwan</i>. The latter part <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> identical with modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">eer</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">before</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">wannehr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb">wéini</i>, obsolete <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wannehe</i>.
</p>

<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a></b>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***wat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> (11)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷód</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷod</i>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">what</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hvad</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_3">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what: e.g. (1) asking for a subject complement; (2) asking for a sentence object
<dl><dd>(1) <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>?</i>  |  <i>What</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that?</dd>
<dd>(2) <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>?</i>  |  <i>What</i> do you want to do?</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what: e.g. (1) as the object of a sentence; (2) ditto
<dl><dd>(1) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i>  |  I don't know <i>what</i> I want to do.</dd>
<dd>(2) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> afblijven <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziet.html>ziet</a>.</i>  |  You must not touch <i>what</i> you see there.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that: e.g. (1) modifying an indefinite pronoun like <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a>; (2) modifying an adjective that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a noun, usually a superlative
<dl><dd>(1) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> eetbaar <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i>  |  Please give <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> everything that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> edible.</dd>
<dd>(2) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> duurste <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i>  |  The most expensive <i>that</i> there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> which: e.g. (1) modifying the demonstrative pronouns <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> and datgene; (2) referring back to an entire sentence
<dl><dd>(1) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nemen.html>nam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a> datgene <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>gewild</a></i>  |  He took exactly that <i>which</i> I <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> wanted.</dd>
<dd>(2) <i>Jantje <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> in z’n broek, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a> in verlegenheid <a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>bracht</a>.</i>  |  John did it in his pants, <i>which</i> embarrassed his mother</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">indefinite</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something: e.g. (1) as subject; (2) as subject complement
<dl><dd>(1) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>loopt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> rond.</i>  |  <i>Something</i> there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> walking around.</dd>
<dd>(2) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardig.html>aardig</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b>!</i>  |  That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> quite <i>something</i>! [i.e. "That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> quite a lot!"]</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This pronoun can combine with a preposition to form a pronominal adverb. When this occurs, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> changed into its adverbial/locative counterpart <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></i>. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p><p>A subclause following the relative pronoun <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in SOV order.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>some
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:graag.html>graag</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> kersen.</i>
<dl><dd>I want <b>some</b> cherries please.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_3">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>a bit, somewhat
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> onbedachtzaam.</i>
<dl><dd>He does that <b>somewhat</b> unthoughtfully.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

***weer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> (116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contracted form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">weder</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">again</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>again
<ul><li><b>1888</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Willem_Kloos" class="extiw" title="w:Willem Kloos">Willem Kloos</a>, “O, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> haten <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergeten.html>vergeten</a>!”
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">In dreigend gillen <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> 'k <b>weêr</b> opgestaan.</span><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Yelling threateningly I rose again.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">nogmaals</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">opnieuw</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">weerom</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>back</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contracted form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">weder</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">weder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wedar</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wedrą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wedʰrom</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>weather</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">weder</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">withar</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wether, ram</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weþruz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wether</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wet-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">year</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>wees</a> (424)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wêse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wēso</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*waiso</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Waise</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">wêse</i>, probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">*wāsa</i> (in <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wuduwāsa</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>wees</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>wezen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>weesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An orphan, who survived both parents</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a> (95)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wech</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">weh</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:weg.html>weg</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wegaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weǵʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***wel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a> (39)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wela</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wala</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wela</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*welh₁-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wohl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">well</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">vel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">väl</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">vel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>The opposite of not (used to add positive emphasis to the verb, much like the auxiliaries "do" or "does" in affirmative sentences in English)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dacht.html>dacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> golf <a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>hield</a>?  |  <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hou.html>hou</a> <b>wél</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> golf!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I thought you didn't like golf?  |  I <b>do</b> like golf!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziet.html>ziet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>...</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">You [can] <b>certainly</b> see that...</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ken.html>ken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>do</b> know him, but not well.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>Maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Well then, what <i><b>do</b></i> you want?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>no less than, as much as, as many as <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">expressing amazement</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> twaalf <a href = vnd.unilang:uur.html>uur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>gewerkt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She has worked <b>no less than</b> twelve hours today!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fairly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voel.html>voel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardig.html>aardig</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I feel <b>fairly</b> decent, but not really good.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> well
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> does, that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>well</b> done.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">"<a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>gedacht</a>," <a href = vnd.unilang:zeggen.html>zeide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">"That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>well</b> thought through, " he said.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>In sense 1, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often strongly stressed (especially when directly contradicting a negative statement or question) and therefore written with an accent: <i>wél</i>.</li>
<li>Using <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> as adverbial form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>goed</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> rare. Usually, the adjective <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in its bare form (as with other adjectives).</li>
<li>The use of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a></i> in the sense of "fairly", while quite idiomatic, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> very unemphatic. When translating to English, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> to leave it out.</li></ul>

***wereld.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a> (283)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">werelt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">werold</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">werolt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weraldiz</i>, from Proto-Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weraz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aldiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">time, age, old</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, hence "age of <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>".
</p><p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wrâld</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">world</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Welt</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">värld</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>werelden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereldje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>world</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The genitive form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">'s werelds</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still in common use.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> (180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">werc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*werką</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wérǵom</i>.

<ol><li>task, job, chore

<li>workplace

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a> (344)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wirken</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wirkijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to work, make</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*werǵ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to work, act</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work, labour</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to work, to be effective</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to function, be in working order</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> amateur radio</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to contact</li></ol>

***weten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a> (139)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wēten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">witan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*witaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wóyde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a root perfect from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyd-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to know (knowledge)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> planeet <a href = vnd.unilang:heet.html>heet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>know</b> what that planet <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> koud <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> vorig <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I still <b>remember</b> how cold it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> last year.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be able to, to manage to (literally, "to know how to/to know of a way to")
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Frisii <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> Germaans volk <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> verscheidene <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> Germaanse volkeren <b><a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>wisten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> fel <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> verdedigen <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Romeinen. <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>Toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeten.html>moesten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Frisii <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> 12 onderwerpen doordat veldheer Drusus <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wist.html>wist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> verslaan.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Frisii were a Germanic people and just like various other Germanic peoples they <b>were able to</b> fiercely defend themselves against the Romans. Nevertheless, the Frisii <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to subject themselves in the year 12 because warlord Drusus <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> able to</b> defeat them.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> voornamelijk <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> lokaal niveau succesvolle partij Freie Wähler <b><a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> deelstaatniveau <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> kiesdrempel <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halen.html>halen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The party Freie Wähler, successful primarily at the local level, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> able</b> for the first time to achieve the election threshold somewhere at the state level.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a> (85)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> subjective or objective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> who, whom
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Who</b>’s there?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezien.html>gezien</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Whom</b> did you see?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> subjective or objective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> who, whom; the one who, whoever
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>Wie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> leest <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> geletterd.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>The one who</b> reads this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> literate.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> receptionist <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wie.html>wie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> pakket <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> afgegeven, <a href = vnd.unilang:werken.html>werkte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The receptionist to <b>whom</b> I handed <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the parcel <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> only recently started working there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> (140)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wi</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wī</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wīz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wéy-</i>, plural of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*éǵh₂</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">wi</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wy</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wir</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">vi</i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> (173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wild</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Inflected form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wild</i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>wilden</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>savage, uncivilized person</li>
<li>brute</li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">brute</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bruut</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">woesteling</span></li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">wildenhorde</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">wildenras</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">weelde</i></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wildi</i>, a contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a> gi</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilt.html>wilt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>gij</a></i>).
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The contraction <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes reinforced with an additional <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>gij</a></i>, giving <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>gij</a></i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zonder.html>zonder</a> beschaving
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> weinig beleefd <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>wilden</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uit.html>uit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maken.html>maken</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li></ol>

***willen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a> (166)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wiljaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*welh₁-</i>. The variant spelling <i><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>wouden</a></i> goes back to early <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wolde</i><i>(n)</i>, following the standard <i>ol</i> gt; <i>ou</i> transformation in Middle Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to want, to desire</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the past tense</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wou.html>wou</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kon.html>kon</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>wish</b> I could (do) that.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wou.html>Wou</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>wouden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often used in the past tense, depending on the region, but mostly in informal language. In formal language, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>wilden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> preferred by many, although <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wou.html>wou</a></i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>wouden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> recognized as correct standard Dutch.
</p>

***worden.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> (123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>werden</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">werthan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*werþaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wértti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become; to get; to grow; to turn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a> lerares <b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She always wanted to become a teacher.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>Mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broer.html>broer</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a> twintig.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">My brother <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> turning twenty today.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> benauwd. Open <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> ramen <a href = vnd.unilang:alsjeblieft.html>alsjeblieft</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">It's getting very stuffy in here. Please open the windows!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form the imperfect tense of the passive voice, together with a past participle.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b> gered.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They are being saved.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> muur <b><a href = vnd.unilang:werd.html>werd</a></b> geschilderd.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The wall <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> being painted.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> muur <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b> geschilderd.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The wall will be painted. / The wall <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> going to be painted.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The perfect tense passive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> formed using <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i>. The form matches English continuous constructions in meaning. Therefore, as in usage 2 above,</li></ul>
<ol><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b> gered.</i> translates to “They <b>are being</b> saved.”</li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>werden</a></b> gered</i>. translates to “They <b>were being</b> saved.”</li>
<li>Consequently, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> </i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></b><i> gered.</i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> </i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a></b><i> gered.</i> would be translated as “They <b>have been</b> saved.” and “They <b><a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> been</b> saved.” respectively.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">verworden</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">wording</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">gewaarworden</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wakker.html>wakker</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i>Werkwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a></b>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">hulpwerkwoord</span> vormt <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> lijdende vorm

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaak.html>zaak</a> (416)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sāke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*saka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sakō</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sake</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">saak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cause; business</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Saak</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Sache</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing; matter; cause; legal cause</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">sag</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">sak</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍃𐌰𐌺𐌾𐍉</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sakjō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dispute, argument</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li>shop, small store, business

***zat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a> (311)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sadaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*seh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zat</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zat.html>zatter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">zatst</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> (14)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_4">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>Unstressed form of <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">feminine singular subject</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There <b>she</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sitting.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Unstressed form of <a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural subject</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zitten.html>zitten</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There <b>they</b> are sitting.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Unstressed form of <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">feminine singular object</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>zie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I see <b>her</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>Unstressed form of <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plural object</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>zie</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I see <b>them</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_3">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In the Netherlands, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a reduced form of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> chiefly when referring to feminine inanimate things:</li></ul>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wist.html>wist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarheid.html>waarheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wilde.html>wilde</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I didn’t know the truth and didn’t wish to know <b>it</b> either.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd>It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often avoided by using the reduced form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">h'r</i> or the masculine form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a></i> or the neuter form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i> or, in formal style, the full form <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i>.</dd></dl>
<ul><li>In Belgium, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usual as a reduced form of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> when referring to persons (as in the example further above).</li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in certain short and idiomatic phrases in the imperative wishing one good luck, the most common by far being <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werk.html>werk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good luck at work!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

***zeggen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeggen.html>zeggen</a> (122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seggen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*seggen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sagjaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sekʷ-</i>. The irregular past tense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a common Ingvaeonic development of the northern dialects, seen also in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">brein</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">zeil</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeggen.html>zeggen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to say, tell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>Als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>beters</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zeggen.html>zeggen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebt.html>hebt</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zeg.html>zeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dan.html>dan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">If you have nothing better to <b>say</b>, then say nothing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zei.html>zei</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>told</b> you so!</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hem.html>hem</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gezegd.html>gezegd</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>told</b> him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The irregular past tense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used in the Netherlands, while the weak past forms are used primarily in Flanders.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeker.html>zeker</a> (147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sēker</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sikur</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*sikur</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">free, secure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sēcūrus</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zelf.html>zelf</a> (262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">self</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">self</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*selvo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*selbaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*selbʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one's own</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*s(w)e-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">separate, apart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">sulv</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">self</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">self</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">selbst</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">selber</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">selv</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intensifier</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> oneself, referring to the subject of a sentence: myself, yourself, itself, ourselves, themselves etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:zelf.html>Zelf</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heen.html>heen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>himself</b> did not go there.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>oneself, by oneself, alone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zelf.html>zelf</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:kun.html>kun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helpen.html>helpen</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I can't do that <b>(by) myself</b>, can you help <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
